creations-chat 2022-10-06 10:18:11 Ok, pro tip. Dont try and link plane crazy to irl, its nothing like that, building mechanics are NOT like how you would actually build a plane. Learn motorlock, piston lock, angle lock and camera lock, look at other peoples builds and you will get inpiration. Use the block select to your advantage. For example, you can use sparklers for turret cannons, or you could use trails. Use signs and text to detail. Make your own colours. NEVER USE LEGACY GLASS.  After all these steps are complete, you are now a plane crazy pro. It is best if you have someone to teach you in game.
